================================================================================
baldur_add

/*
    If PC is a non-Lawful Wild Mage, he spontaneously casts a spell when he loses 50% of his hitpoints.
*/

IF
  Global("wm_spellshaper", "GLOBAL", 0)
  !Alignment(Player1, MASK_LAWFUL)
  Class(Player1, MAGE)
  Kit(Player1, 0)
  HPPercentLT(Player1, 51)
  NotStateCheck(Player1, STATE_HELPLESS)
  NotStateCheck(Player1, STATE_STUNNED)
  NotStateCheck(Player1, STATE_PANIC)
  NotStateCheck(Player1, STATE_BERSERK)
  NotStateCheck(Player1, STATE_SLEEPING)
  NotStateCheck(Player1, STATE_CHARMED)
  NotStateCheck(Player1, STATE_CONFUSED)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    ActionOverride(Player1, ForceSpell(LastAttackerOf(Myself), WIZARD_LARLOCH_MINOR_DRAIN))
    SmallWait(15)
    SetGlobal("wm_spellshaper", "GLOBAL", 1)
    ActionOverride(Player1, StartDialog("WM_LEVEL", Myself))
END

//-------------------------------
// After Resting: Rhialto appears
//-------------------------------

IF
  Global("wm_start", "GLOBAL", 0)
  Global("wm_bg1book", "GLOBAL", 0)   // Do not appear in BG2 if already appeared in BG1 part
  Global("wm_bg1bear", "GLOBAL", 0)   // Do not appear in BG2 if already appeared in BG1 part
  GlobalGT("Chapter", "GLOBAL", 0)
  PartyRested()
  AreaType(OUTDOOR)
//  Class(Player1,MAGE)
//  Kit(Player1,WILDMAGE)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    ActionOverride(Player1, CreateCreature("wm_rhia1", [-1.-1], 0))
    SetGlobal("wm_start", "GLOBAL", 1)
    Continue()
END

detection

// normal detection
IF
  Detected([ANYONE])
  // %is_active%
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    SetGlobal("%trap_var_base%_detected", "MYAREA", 1)
    Continue()
END

// instant detection
IF
  // %traps_baf_instant_toggle%
  Global("%trap_var_base%_detected", "MYAREA", 0)
  // %is_active%
  // %traps_baf_class%
  // %traps_baf_range%
  !StateCheck(LastSeenBy, CD_STATE_NOTVALID)
  !CheckStatLT(LastSeenBy, %detection%, TRAPS)
  TriggerOverride(LastSeenBy, ModalState(DETECTTRAPS))
  ActionListEmpty()
THEN
  RESPONSE #1
    ReallyForceSpellRES("%trap_spl%", Myself)
    SetGlobal("%trap_var_base%_detected", "MYAREA", 1)
    Continue()
END

================================================================================
displaystring
================================================================================

// Display detected trap type
IF
  Global("%trap_var_base%_detected", "MYAREA", 1) // has been detected with thief's skill
  Global("%trap_var_base%_disarmed", "MYAREA", 0) // hasn't been disarmed or set off
  !GlobalTimerNotExpired("%trap_var_base%_timer", "MYAREA") // don't spam the dialog box
  // %is_active%
  // %traps_baf_combat%
  Detect([PC])
  // %traps_baf_range%
  ActionListEmpty()
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    SetGlobalTimer("%trap_var_base%_timer", "MYAREA", %notification_delay%)
    // Using a minion for DisplayString allows to put the notification into the center of the trap.
    // If calling DisplayString directly from trap script, it's off, and sometimes very much off, misleading the player.
    CreateCreatureImpassableAllowOverlap("%traps_minion_notification%", [%x%.%y%], 0)
    DisplayStringNoNameHead("%traps_minion_notification%", ~%trap_warning_string%~)
    // %ee_trap_type_string_delay% // On EE, DisplayStringNoNameHead disappears nearly instantly
    ActionOverride("%traps_minion_notification%", DestroySelf())
    Continue()
END

/* Do not edit. This file is generated from g_fam.tbaf. Make your changes there and regenerate this file. */

IF
  G("g_FamJumpToPack", 1)
  OR(2)
    !CombatCounterLT(1)
    See([EVILCUTOFF])
  !Dead("%death_var%")
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    MoveToObject(Player1)
    GiveItemCreate("%fam_item%", Player1, 0, 0, 0)
    DestroySelf()
END

  OR(4)
    See(NearestEnemyOfType([0.GENERAL_ITEM.0.MAGE_ALL]))

    See(NearestEnemyOfType([0.GENERAL_ITEM.0.DRUID_ALL]))

// Initial PI spy script.
// Its only purpose is to get clone creature into LastHeard, then pass management to the main script.
IF
  Heard([ANYONE], %g_pnp_pi_shout%)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    // DisplayStringHead(Myself, ~spy heard~)
    ChangeAIScript("g_pispy1", OVERRIDE)
    // DisplayStringHead(Myself, ~spy changed~)
END
// IF
//   OnCreation()
// THEN
//   RESPONSE #100
//     DisplayStringHead(Myself, ~spy created~)
// END
// IF
//   True()
// THEN
//   RESPONSE #100
//     DisplayStringHead(Myself, ~spy waiting~)
//     Continue()
// END

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

(source_file
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (block
    if: (if_clause
      (condition
        call: (call_expr
          func: (identifier)
          args: (object_ref)
          args: (variable_ref))))
    then: (then_clause
      (response
        weight: (number)
        (line_comment)
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier)
            args: (string)
            args: (identifier)))))
    (line_comment))
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)

g_pispy1
================================================================================

// Main PI spy script.
// It tracks spells cast by the clone, sets local variables, then removes them one by one and once all is clear, destroys itself.
// The grunt work is APPENDed later in main.tpa

IF
  Global("interrupt_set", "LOCALS", 0)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    SetInterrupt(FALSE) // just in case
    SetGlobal("interrupt_set", "LOCALS", 1)
END
IF
  !Exists(LastHeardBy)
  // %final_check_list%
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    ActionOverride(LastSummonerOf, SetInterrupt(TRUE))
    DestroySelf()
END
// IF
//   True()
// THEN
//   RESPONSE #100
//     DisplayStringHead(LastHeardBy, ~I am projected image~)
//     DisplayStringHead(LastSummonerOf, ~I am original~)
//     DisplayStringHead(Myself, ~pi checking spells~)
//     Continue()
// END

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

(source_file
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (block
    if: (if_clause
      (condition
        call: (call_expr
          func: (identifier)
          args: (string)
          args: (string)
          args: (number))))
    then: (then_clause
      (response
        weight: (number)
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier)
            args: (identifier)))
        (line_comment)
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier)
            args: (string)
            args: (string)
            args: (number))))))
  (block
    if: (if_clause
      (condition
        call: (call_expr
          func: (identifier)
          args: (identifier))))
    (line_comment)
    then: (then_clause
      (response
        weight: (number)
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier)
            args: (identifier)
            args: (call_expr
              func: (identifier)
              args: (identifier))))
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier))))))
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment))

================================================================================
g_pispy1_spell_block
================================================================================

// Individual spell blocks for each spell.
// Local vars track how many times the spell was cast.
// Some spell ids are too long for a var name, so have to use spell resource instead.

IF
  SpellCast(LastHeardBy, %spell%)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    IncrementGlobal("%spell_res%", "LOCALS", 1)
    // DisplayStringHead(Myself, ~Detected cast: %spell%~)
END
IF
  GlobalGT("%spell_res%", "LOCALS", 0)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    IncrementGlobal("%spell_res%", "LOCALS", -1)
    ActionOverride(LastSummonerOf, SetInterrupt(FALSE))
    ActionOverride(LastSummonerOf, RemoveSpellRES("%spell_res%"))
    // ActionOverride(LastSummonerOf, DisplayStringHead(Myself, ~Removed %spell_res%~))
END

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

(source_file
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (line_comment)
  (block
    if: (if_clause
      (condition
        call: (call_expr
          func: (identifier)
          args: (identifier)
          args: (variable_ref))))
    then: (then_clause
      (response
        weight: (number)
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier)
            args: (string)
            args: (string)
            args: (number)))))
    (line_comment))
  (block
    if: (if_clause
      (condition
        call: (call_expr
          func: (identifier)
          args: (string)
          args: (string)
          args: (number))))
    then: (then_clause
      (response
        weight: (number)
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier)
            args: (string)
            args: (string)
            args: (number)))
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier)
            args: (identifier)
            args: (call_expr
              func: (identifier)
              args: (identifier))))
        (action
          call: (call_expr
            func: (identifier)
            args: (identifier)
            args: (call_expr
              func: (identifier)
              args: (string))))))
    (line_comment)))

// PI clone script. Assigned by projimag.spl.

  OnCreation()
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    GlobalShout(%g_pnp_pi_shout%)
    // DisplayStringHead(Myself, ~pi shouted~)
END

================================================================================
intuition
================================================================================

// intuition main action
IF
  Global("%trap_var_base%_detected", "MYAREA", 0)
  Global("%trap_var_base%_disarmed", "MYAREA", 0)
  !GlobalTimerNotExpired("%intuition_timer%", "MYAREA") // don't spam the actions
  // %is_active%
  // %traps_baf_combat%
  Detect([PC])
  // %traps_baf_range%
  !StateCheck(LastSeenBy, CD_STATE_NOTVALID)
  ActionListEmpty()
THEN
  RESPONSE #1
    SetGlobal("%trap_var_base%_intuition", "MYAREA", 1)
    // SetGlobalTimer("%intuition_timer%", "MYAREA", %intuition_delay%)
    Continue()
END

// intuition: character strings
IF
  Global("%trap_var_base%_intuition", "MYAREA", 1)
  ActionListEmpty()
THEN
  RESPONSE #1

IF
  Global("%trap_var_base%_intuition", "MYAREA", 1)
THEN
  RESPONSE #1
    // %traps_baf_view%
    Continue()
END

// intuition: sound
IF
  // %traps_baf_sound_toggle%
  Global("%trap_var_base%_intuition", "MYAREA", 1)
THEN
  RESPONSE #1
    PlaySound("act_09")
    Continue()
END

// intuition: autopause
IF
  // %traps_baf_pause_toggle%
  Global("%trap_var_base%_intuition", "MYAREA", 1)
  !GlobalTimerNotExpired("%pause_timer%", "GLOBAL") // don't spam pause, global timer in case there's multiple traps in sight
THEN
  RESPONSE #1
    // SetGlobalTimer("%pause_timer%", "GLOBAL", %pause_delay%)
    ActionOverride(LastSeenBy, PauseGame()) // interrupts player orders
    Continue()
END

// intuition: start searching for traps - after pause because pausing interrupts modal actions too
IF
  // %traps_baf_force_find_traps_toggle%
  Global("%trap_var_base%_intuition", "MYAREA", 1)
  Global("%trap_var_base%_detected", "MYAREA", 0)
  // %traps_baf_class%
  // %traps_baf_range%
  // %is_active%
  !StateCheck(LastSeenBy, CD_STATE_NOTVALID)
  // !CheckStatLT(LastSeenBy, %detection%, TRAPS)
  !TriggerOverride(LastSeenBy, ModalState(DETECTTRAPS))
  // we don't want thieves coming out of stealth automatically, there could be enemies present
  !TriggerOverride(LastSeenBy, ModalState(STEALTH))
THEN
  RESPONSE #1
    ActionOverride(LastSeenBy, FindTraps())
    Continue()
END

// end intuition
IF
  Global("%trap_var_base%_intuition", "MYAREA", 1)
THEN
  RESPONSE #1
    SetGlobal("%trap_var_base%_intuition", "MYAREA", 0)
    Continue()
END

// Automatically jump out of backpack if directed to do so.
// Goes to baldur/baldur25.bcs.

IF
    Global("g_FamiliarJumpOut", "GLOBAL", 1)
    Global("g_FamStayInPack", "GLOBAL", 0)
    HasItem("%fam_item%", Player1)
    Delay(12)  // check every 2 rounds
    CombatCounterLT(1)
    !OnScreen([EVILCUTOFF])
    NextTriggerObject(Player1)
    !Detect([EVILCUTOFF])
THEN
    RESPONSE #100
        TakePartyItem("%fam_item%")
        DestroyItem("%fam_item%")
        MoveGlobalObject("%death_var%", Player1)
        Continue()
END

//Start warning again when reset
IF
  Reset([ANYONE])
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    SetGlobal("%trap_var_base%_disarmed", "MYAREA", 0)
    Continue()
END

//Stop warning when fired
IF
  OR(3)
    Disarmed([ANYONE])
    Opened([ANYONE])  // for containers
    Entered([ANYONE])  // for regions
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    SetGlobal("%trap_var_base%_disarmed", "MYAREA", 1)
    Continue()
END

// ----------------------------------------------------
//   Force-equip "Chaos Stuff"-Item (After Spell)
// ----------------------------------------------------
IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", 0)
  ActionListEmpty()
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    Face(0)
    SmallWait(10)
    ClearAllActions()
    CutSceneId(Myself)
    StartCutSceneMode()
    ScreenShake([10.10], 20)
    PlayDead(15)
    ApplySpellRES("WM_CHAO", Myself)
    ReallyForceSpellRES("wm_shear", Myself)
    DropInventory()
    DisplayStringHead(Myself, @20111)
    PlayDead(350)
    GiveItemCreate("wm_chaos", Myself, 1, 1, 0)
    FillSlot(SLOT_RING_LEFT)
    PlaySound("EFF_M20")
    ApplySpellRES("SPWM134", Myself)    // Wild Magic: "Bird Magic"
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -1)
    DisplayStringHead(Myself, @20112)
    Wait(5)
    EndCutSceneMode()
    Continue()
END

// ----------------------------------------------------
//   Force-equip "Chaos Stuff"-Item (Spontaneous)
// ----------------------------------------------------
IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -10)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    ApplySpellRES("WM_CHAO", Myself)
    ForceSpellRES("wm_shear", Myself)
    SmallWait(5)
    ScreenShake([10.10], 20)
    DropInventory()
    PlayDead(6)
    GiveItemCreate("wm_chaos", Myself, 1, 1, 0)
    FillSlot(SLOT_RING_LEFT)
    PlaySound("EFF_M20")
    ApplySpellRES("SPWM134", Myself)    // Wild Magic: "Bird Magic"
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -1)
    SmallWait(10)
    Continue()
END

// ----------------------------------------------------
//         Force Alignment: CHAOTIC
// ----------------------------------------------------

IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -1)
  Alignment(Myself, MASK_GOOD)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    ChangeAlignment(Myself, CHAOTIC_GOOD)
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -2)
    Continue()
END

IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -1)
  Alignment(Myself, MASK_GENEUTRAL)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    ChangeAlignment(Myself, CHAOTIC_NEUTRAL)
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -2)
    Continue()
END

IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -1)
  Alignment(Myself, MASK_EVIL)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    ChangeAlignment(Myself, CHAOTIC_EVIL)
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -2)
    Continue()
END


// ----------------------------------------------------
//         Change Avatar
// ----------------------------------------------------

IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -2)
  Gender(Myself, MALE)
  Race(Myself, HUMAN)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    Polymorph(CLERIC_MALE_HUMAN)
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -3)
END

IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -2)
  Gender(Myself, MALE)
  OR(2)
    Race(Myself, ELF)
    Race(Myself, HALF_ELF)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    Polymorph(CLERIC_MALE_ELF)
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -3)
END

IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -2)
  Gender(Myself, FEMALE)
  Race(Myself, HUMAN)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    Polymorph(THIEF_FEMALE_HUMAN)
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -3)
END

IF
   Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -2)
  Gender(Myself, FEMALE)
  OR(2)
    Race(Myself, ELF)
    Race(Myself, HALF_ELF)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    Polymorph(THIEF_FEMALE_ELF)
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", -3)
END


// ----------------------------------------------------
//         Wait till initialized
// ----------------------------------------------------

IF
  Global("wm_level", "LOCALS", -3)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    SelectWeaponAbility(SLOT_WEAPON0, 0)
    AddSpecialAbility("wm_weave")       // Weave
    AddSpecialAbility("wm_shear")       // Weaveshear
    ChangeAIScript("wm_chaos", OVERRIDE)
    StartDialog("WM_LEVEL", Myself)     // Select Feat
    SetDialog("")
    SetGlobal("wm_level", "LOCALS", 1)
END

================================================================================
wm_disp
================================================================================

IF
  Global("gone","LOCALS",1)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    NoAction()
END

IF
  True()
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    SetGlobal("gone","LOCALS",1)
    Continue()
END


IF
  Inparty(Myself)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    LeaveParty()
    Continue()
END

IF
  !Allegiance(Myself,Enemy)
THEN
  RESPONSE #100
    Help()
    Shout(99)     // Non-Enemies, even party members, alert guards...
    Continue()
END

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    AddexperienceParty(10)
    Destroyself()
